HL7 - Mean? "Level Seven" refers seventh level International Organization Standardization (ISO) seven-layer communication model Open Systems Interconnection (OSI) - application level. application level interface directly performs common application service application processes. HL7 encompasses complete life cycle standard specification including development, adoption, market recognition, utilization, adherence. Please refer information member non-members use standards. Product Grid includes Products Active Stable status life cycle. Retired standard available . lifecycle status defined as: Active: standard ha published, known planned use, planned future maintenance releases. Stable: standard may use may generate feedback questions, active review, expected updated foreseeable future. Retired: standard ha current planned standard development activity within community; may longer use, considered use.
